 I have received following reply from Amazon. Hope this helps. \r<br />\r<br />Item is covered by a standard Amazon two year warranty - if the item develops fault in this period, you can always return it to us and get a replacement (if the item is on stock) or full refund for it.\r&hellip;\n        <a aria-label=\"Hier klicken, um den Inhalt zu einzublenden.\" class=\"a-link-normal askSeeMore\" href=\"#\">\n          Weitere Informationen\n        </a>\n      </span>\n      <span class=\"askLongText\">\n        I have received following reply from Amazon. Hope this helps. \r<br />\r<br />Item is covered by a standard Amazon two year warranty - if the item develops fault in this period, you can always return it to us and get a replacement (if the item is on stock) or full refund for it.\r<br />\r<br />After expiration of the warranty, you can contact the local representative of the manufacturer and try to claim manufacturer's warranty (depending on the item, it can vary between 2-5 years - some items have a lifetime warranty).\r<br />\r<br />When it comes to returning the defective item to us, we will provide you the assistance on your request - you can either call us or send us an e-mail, explain the fault and state your request (replacement  / refund) and then we would provide you with return label.\r<br />\r<br />Considering that you plan to order this item and deliver it to an address in Sweden, that would be standard, non-prepaid return label - you would have to choose any local carrier and pay for the return shipping. Then you would have to provide us with the picture of the return shipping receipt that you received from the carrier and a tracking ID - based on it, Amazon will gladly refund you for return shipping.\n        <a aria-label=\"Hier klicken, um den Text zu minimieren.\" class=\"a-link-normal askSeeLess\" href=\"#\">\n          Weniger anzeigen\n        </a>\n      </span>\n    </span>\n    <span class=\"noScriptDisplayLongText\">\n      <span>I have received following reply from Amazon. Hope this helps. \r<br />\r<br />Item is covered by a standard Amazon two year warranty - if the item develops fault in this period, you can always return it to us and get a replacement (if the item is on stock) or full refund for it.\r<br />\r<br />After expiration of the warranty, you can contact the local representative of the manufacturer and try to claim manufacturer's warranty (depending on the item, it can vary between 2-5 years - some items have a lifetime warranty).\r<br />\r<br />When it comes to returning the defective item to us, we will provide you the assistance on your request - you can either call us or send us an e-mail, explain the fault and state your request (replacement  / refund) and then we would provide you with return label.\r<br />\r<br />Considering that you plan to order this item and deliver it to an address in Sweden, that would be standard, non-prepaid return label - you would have to choose any local carrier and pay for the return shipping. Then you would have to provide us with the picture of the return shipping receipt that you received from the carrier and a tracking ID - based on it, Amazon will gladly refund you for return shipping.</span>\n    </span>\n  \n  \n\n                <br/>\n\n                \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n    <div class=\"a-section a-spacing-none a-spacing-top-micro\">\n      <a href=\"/gp/profile/amzn1.account.AHYZKBWZR2CDJSBYKGJU7IL32VSA/ref=ask_ql_ql_pp_hza\" class=\"a-profile aok-inline-block aok-align-center ask-profile-avatar-normal\" data-a-size=\"small\"><div aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"a-profile-avatar-wrapper\"><div class=\"a-profile-avatar\"><img src=\"/avatar/default/amzn1.account.AHYZKBWZR2CDJSBYKGJU7IL32VSA?square=true&amp;max_width=48\"/></div></div><div class=\"a-profile-content\"><span class=\"a-profile-name\">Sac</span></div></a>\n      <span class=\"a-color-tertiary aok-align-center\">\n        &#183 15.
